<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:азиатский.html>азиа́тский</a> (9531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:азиат.html>азиа́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aziát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:азиатский.html>азиа́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aziátskij</span>)
</p>

***айда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a> (17338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Supposedly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">әйдә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">äydä</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly related to hajde.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ajdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> let's go, c'mon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xvátit rabótatʹ, <b>ajdá</b> po domám</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Enough of the work, let's go home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:футбол.html>футбо́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ajdá</b> v futból.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's play football.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> made off; dashed away; vanished
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поругаться.html>поруга́лись</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещичка.html>вещи́чки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My porugálisʹ, on sobrál veščíčki i <b>ajdá</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We had a quarrel, then he got his belongings and left.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>Айда́</a></b> is used mostly as an imperative verb, but it is invariable. In Russian grammar <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> does not count as a true verb and is considered to be closer to an interjection (<a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тие</a>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***академия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a> (2652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akadémija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>academy</li>
<li>college
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Akadémija</b> naúk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Academy of Sciences</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:художество.html>худо́жеств</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Akadémija</b> xudóžestv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Academy of Arts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vojénnaja <b>akadémija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Military College</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">вое́нно-возду́шная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vojénno-vozdúšnaja <b>akadémija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Air Force College</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">вое́нно-медици́нская <b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vojénno-medicínskaja <b>akadémija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Army Medical College</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">вое́нно-морска́я <b><a href = vnd.unilang:академия.html>акаде́мия</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vojénno-morskája <b>akadémija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Naval College</span></div></dd>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Akazie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">acacia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀκακία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akakía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акация.html>ака́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акация.html>ака́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акация.html>ака́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:акация.html>ака́ций</a></b>)
</p>

***аккомпанировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировать.html>аккомпани́ровать</a> (28295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировать.html>аккомпани́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkompanírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">саккомпани́ровать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проаккомпани́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to accompany (to perform an accompanying part next to another instrument)</li></ol>

***аккредитовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккредитовать.html>аккредитова́ть</a> (30126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">akredytować</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">accréditer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккредитовать.html>аккредитова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkreditovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to accredit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to send with letters credential, as an ambassador, envoy, or diplomatic agent; to authorize, as a messenger or delegate.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***аккумулятор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккумулятор.html>аккумуля́тор</a> (3443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккумулятор.html>аккумуля́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkumuljátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккумулятор.html>аккумуля́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккумулятор.html>аккумуля́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккумулятор.html>аккумуля́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>accumulator, (car) battery</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">накопи́тель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakopítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***аккуратно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратно.html>аккура́тно</a> (2381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akkurátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратно.html>аккура́тно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>neatly, smartly</li>
<li>carefully, cautiously, prudently</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратно.html>аккура́тно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akkurátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тностей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a> (4757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">accūrātus</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)аккура́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)аккура́тней</b>)

***аконит.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аконит.html>акони́т</a> (24973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аконит.html>акони́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akonít</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аконит.html>акони́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аконит.html>акони́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аконит.html>акони́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wolfsbane, aconite</li></ol>
